        (fc2): Linear(in_features=2048, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (final_layer_norm): LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      )
    )
    (output_projection): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=26336, bias=False)
  )
)
